; construct constant table
	lda #$02 ;display pointer
	sta $03
	lda #$c3; video pointer - MAGIC NUMBER
	sta $00
	lda #$06 ; data page
	sta $01
	jmp main
	
; use y register for screen px
; use (VIDPOINT) for data pointer
; detect next frame by y overflow
; x must always be zero

main:
	lda ($00,x)
	and #$01
	beq px1
	lda #$01
	sta ($02),y
	jmp ps1
px1:
	lda #$00
	sta ($02),y
ps1:
	iny
		
	lda ($00,x)
	and #$02
	beq px2
	lda #$01
	sta ($02),y
	jmp ps2
px2:
	lda #$00
	sta ($02),y
ps2:
	iny
	
	lda ($00,x)
	and #$04
	beq px3
	lda #$01
	sta ($02),y
	jmp ps3
px3:
	lda #$00
	sta ($02),y
ps3:
	iny
	
	lda ($00,x)
	and #$08
	beq px4
	lda #$01
	sta ($02),y
	jmp ps4
px4:
	lda #$00
	sta ($02),y
ps4:
	iny
	
	lda ($00,x)
	and #$10
	beq px5
	lda #$01
	sta ($02),y
	jmp ps5
px5:
	lda #$00
	sta ($02),y
ps5:
	iny
	
	lda ($00,x)
	and #$20
	beq px6
	lda #$01
	sta ($02),y
	jmp ps6
px6:
	lda #$00
	sta ($02),y
ps6:
	iny
	
	lda ($00,x)
	and #$40
	beq px7
	lda #$01
	sta ($02),y
	jmp ps7
px7:
	lda #$00
	sta ($02),y
ps7:
	iny
	
	lda ($00,x)
	and #$80
	beq px8
	lda #$01
	sta ($02),y
	jmp ps8
px8:
	lda #$00
	sta ($02),y
ps8:
	iny
	; check display page
	bne nbyte
	inc $03
	lda #$06
	cmp $03
	bne nbyte
	lda #$02
	sta $03
	;frame delay
	lda #$00
delay:
	adc #$01
	cmp #$55
	bne delay
	inx
	bne delay
	clc
nbyte:	
	;next byte
	inc $00
	bne stp
	inc $01
stp:jmp main
	brk
vid:
dcb
